Test 1: [network-flow-matrix-tests] telco5g-network-flow-matrix-bm-network-flow-matrix-tests container test

• Duration: 72s
• Error: error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git (after silent API server timeout)
• Evidence:

```

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64414: i/o timeout

Cloning into '/tmp/secret/commatrix'...

/tmp/secret/commatrix /

error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git

```

• Root Cause: The cluster API at 10.1.104.200:64414 was unreachable when the test container started. The test script network-flow-matrix-tests-commands.sh calls get_cluster_version() which runs oc version | grep "Server Version:" — when oc version fails silently, version is empty, major and minor are both empty strings, so cluster_version evaluates to . (just a period), and testing_branch="release-$cluster_version" becomes release-.. The branch release-. does not exist; the valid branch release-4.21 does exist in openshift-kni/commatrix. The first domino is the unreachable API server (10.1.104.200:64414), not a code regression.
• Breaking PR/Commit: The release-. bug is a latent scripting bug in [network-flow-matrix-tests-commands.sh](https://github.com/openshift/release/blob/main/ci-operator/step-registry/network-flow-matrix/tests/network-flow-matrix-tests-commands.sh) (lines 4–12) — it is only triggered when oc version fails. The cluster API going down is an infra event with Unknown commit/cause.
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift/release/blob/main/ci-operator/step-registry/network-flow-matrix/tests/network-flow-matrix-tests-commands.sh
• Is it a flake? Yes — cluster API unreachability is a transient infra failure; the cascaded git-checkout failure is masked by the same root cause.
• Suggested Fix: Add set -e guard or explicit check on oc version exit code in get_cluster_version(): if oc version fails, exit with a clear error instead of silently continuing with an empty version string.

Test 1: network-flow-matrix-tests — main test step

• Duration: 71s
• Error: error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git (exit code 1)
• Evidence:

```

Unable to connect to the server: dial tcp 10.1.104.200:64415: i/o timeout

Cloning into '/tmp/secret/commatrix'...

/tmp/secret/commatrix /

error: pathspec 'release-.' did not match any file(s) known to git

{"component":"entrypoint","error":"wrapped process failed: exit status 1",...}

```

• Root Cause: The cluster API server at 10.1.104.200:64415 was unreachable before the test script ran. The network-flow-matrix-tests-commands.sh script calls get_cluster_version() which runs oc version | grep "Server Version:" | awk '{print $3}' — because the API was down this returns empty string, so major="", minor="", and the function echoes "$major.$minor" → ".". Then testing_branch="release-$cluster_version" → "release-.". git checkout release-. fails because no such branch exists. The first domino is the unreachable API server.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra failure, not a code regression
• Source File: [network-flow-matrix-tests-commands.sh (steps registry)](https://steps.ci.openshift.org/reference/network-flow-matrix-tests)
• Is it a flake? No — cluster API server unreachability is an infra fault, not a transient test issue.
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. If recurrent, investigate the telco5g-cluster-setup step: the cluster setup reported success after 1h55m but the API server became unreachable immediately after. Add a guard in get_cluster_version() to exit non-zero if oc version fails, so the error is clear rather than manifesting as a bad branch name.

• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix (tests never ran)
• Is it a flake? yes — same infra root cause
• Suggested Fix: Same as Test 1.

I now have all the evidence needed. Let me write the analysis.



Test 1: [telco5g-sno-setup] RETRYING: [XXXXXXXXXXXX]: Run oc command to check if cluster is ready (60 retries left).

• Duration: ~9209s (2h33m49s total for the setup step)
• Error: OCP API server unreachable — dial tcp 192.168.17.114:6443: connect: no route to host
• Evidence:

> E0617 12:02:25.092451 3747229 memcache.go:265] couldn't get current server API group list: Get "https://api.cnfdu7.upstreamci.bos2.lab:6443/api?timeout=32s": dial tcp 192.168.17.114:6443: connect: no route to host

> PLAY RECAP: XXXXXXXXXXXX: ok=0 changed=0 unreachable=0 failed=1 skipped=0 rescued=0 ignored=0

• Root Cause: The bare-metal SNO node for cluster cnfdu7 failed to complete OCP installation. After ~2.5 hours, the ocp-install.yml Ansible playbook's cluster-readiness oc check hit "no route to host" on the kube-apiserver (192.168.17.114:6443), indicating the node lost network routing or the OCP bootstrap/install process failed before the API came up. This is a hardware/infra-level failure in the telco5g lab, not a commatrix code issue.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — infra failure, no code involved
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix (commatrix tests never ran)
• Is it a flake? yes — SNO bare-metal install failures due to routing loss are known transient lab infrastructure issues
• Suggested Fix: Retry the job. If persistent, investigate the bare-metal node cnfdu7 for network/BMC issues and confirm the SNO installer can reach the bootstrap host.

• Evidence:

```

Processing monitorTest: pathological-event-analyzer

finalIntervals size = 129054

first interval time: From = 2026-06-21 19:15:28 +0000 UTC; To = 2026-06-21 20:59:35.265698617 +0000 UTC m=+282.951834255

```

And from the network-flow-matrix build log (commatrix nftables test, which ran before this step):

```

2026/06/21 19:45:37 Waiting for node ip-10-0-8-48.us-west-2.compute.internal to be in NotReady state

2026/06/21 19:45:54 Node ip-10-0-8-48.us-west-2.compute.internal is NotReady

```

• Root Cause: The commatrix nftables test (test/e2e/nftables_test.go:85) intentionally reboots the SNO node to verify that nftables firewall rules persist across reboots — this is expected test behavior. The node-not-ready window (19:15:28–20:59:35) also covers the SNO upgrade reboot (upgrade completed at 19:42:34). The subsequent single-node-e2e-test step's pathological-event-analyzer MonitorTest captured this node-not-ready interval as a failure even though all 1943 openshift-tests passed. The ComMatrix project's own step (network-flow-matrix-tests) completed with "passed":true,"result":"SUCCESS".
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — no regression in commatrix code; this is CI framework behavior
• Source File: https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/nftables_test.go#L85
• Is it a flake? Yes — MonitorTest flagging node-not-ready on an SNO upgrade job (where node reboots are intentional) is a known CI framework false positive pattern
• Suggested Fix: The pathological-event-analyzer MonitorTest should allow-list node-not-ready events that are associated with intentional reboots triggered by MCO (MachineConfig Operator) updates or upgrade steps. Alternatively, the commatrix nftables test could annotate/fence its reboot window so MonitorTests skip that interval.


Project test step result: {"passed":true,"result":"SUCCESS"} (network-flow-matrix-tests finished.json)

• Root Cause: PROJECT TESTS PASSED — failure is from CI framework. The commatrix network-flow-matrix-tests step completed successfully (Ginkgo: 1 Passed | 0 Failed). That step intentionally rebooted master-0 at 20:35:21 Z to verify nftables rules survive reboot; the node went NotReady at 20:36:13 Z and recovered by 20:39:36 Z. The subsequent baremetalds-e2e-test step runs the general OpenShift conformance suite on a cluster that had just executed an upgrade and a deliberate control-plane node reboot. The CRDValidationRatcheting blocking failure and the 10 OVN-OTE informing failures are unrelated to commatrix logic — they reflect residual cluster state disruption from the upgrade+reboot sequence.
• Breaking PR/Commit: Unknown — these are OpenShift conformance / OVN-Kubernetes tests, not commatrix code.
• Source File: Commatrix nftables test: [test/e2e/nftables_test.go](https://github.com/openshift-kni/commatrix/blob/main/test/e2e/nftables_test.go) (line 85). The failing conformance tests live in [openshift/openshift-tests](https://github.com/openshift/openshift-tests), not commatrix.
• Is it a flake? yes — [ovn-kubernetes-ote] tests are experimental/OTE-tagged (known flaky); the CRDValidationRatcheting failure on an upgrade-freshly-rebooted cluster is consistent with transient API server state.
• Suggested Fix: No commatrix code change needed. Retry the job; if CRDValidationRatcheting keeps blocking, file an issue against openshift/openshift-tests for post-upgrade cluster state sensitivity.
